**v45** But righteous men will sentence them to the punishment of those who commit adultery and bloodshed, because they are adulteresses with blood on their hands.

**v46** This is what the Lord GOD says: 'Bring a mob against them and consign them to terror and plunder.
**v47** The mob will stone them and cut them down with their swords. They will kill their sons and daughters and burn down their houses.
**v48** So I will put an end to indecency in the land, and all the women will be admonished not to imitate your behavior.
**v49** They will repay you for your indecency, and you will bear the consequences of your sins of idolatry. Then you will know that I am the Lord GOD.'"
[^1]: Oholah means her own tent or she worships at a tent shrine, a metaphor for Samaria as an adulteress with Assyria. ( 23:4)
[^2]: Oholibah means the tent is in her or she is a tent shrine, a metaphor for Jerusalem as an adulterous wife. ( 23:4)
[^3]: That is, the Babylonians ( 23:14)
[^4]: Or Babylonia; also in verse 16 ( 23:15)
[^5]: LXX They will all come against you from the north ( 23:24)
[^6]: Literally passed their children, whom they bore to Me, through the fire ( 23:37)
[^7]: Hebrew they sent ( 23:40)
[^8]: Or Sabeans ( 23:42)

### Chapter 24

#### The Parable of the Cooking Pot
**v1** In the ninth year, on the tenth day of the tenth month, the word of the LORD came to me, saying,
**v2** "Son of man, write down today's date, for on this very day the king of Babylon has laid siege to Jerusalem.
**v3** Now speak a parable to this rebellious house and tell them that this is what the Lord GOD says: 'Put the pot on the fire; put it on and pour in the water.
**v4** Put in the pieces of meat, every good piece—thigh and shoulder—fill it with choice bones.
**v5** Take the choicest of the flockand pile the fuel beneath it.Bring it to a boiland cook the bones in it.'

**v6** Therefore this is what the Lord GOD says: 'Woe to the city of bloodshed, to the pot now rusted, whose rust will not come off!Empty it piece by piece; cast no lots for its contents. [^1]
**v7** For the blood she shed is still within her; she poured it out on the bare rock; she did not pour it on the groundto cover it with dust.
**v8** In order to stir up wrathand take vengeance, I have placed her blood on the bare rock, so that it would not be covered.'

**v9** Yes, this is what the Lord GOD says: 'Woe to the city of bloodshed!I, too, will pile the kindling high.
**v10** Pile on the logs and kindle the fire; cook the meat welland mix in the spices; let the bones be burned.
**v11** Set the empty pot on its coalsuntil it becomes hot and its copper glows.Then its impurity will melt within; its rust will be consumed.
**v12** It has frustrated every effort; its thick rust has not been removed, even by the fire.
**v13** Because of the indecency of your uncleanness I tried to cleanse you, but you would not be purifiedfrom your filthiness.You will not be pure againuntil My wrath against you has subsided.
**v14** I, the LORD, have spoken; the time is coming, and I will act.I will not refrain or show pity, nor will I relent.I will judge youaccording to your ways and deeds,'declares the Lord GOD."
#### Ezekiel's Wife Dies

**v15** Then the word of the LORD came to me, saying,
**v16** "Son of man, behold, I am about to take away the desire of your eyes with a fatal blow. But you must not mourn or weep or let your tears flow.
**v17** Groan quietly; do not mourn for the dead. Put on your turban and strap your sandals on your feet; do not cover your lips or eat the bread of mourners."

**v18** So I spoke to the people in the morning, and in the evening my wife died. And the next morning I did as I had been commanded.

**v19** Then the people asked me, "Won't you tell us what these things you are doing mean to us?"

**v20** So I answered them, "The word of the LORD came to me, saying:
**v21** Tell the house of Israel that this is what the Lord GOD says: 'I am about to desecrate My sanctuary, the pride of your power, the desire of your eyes, and the delight of your soul. And the sons and daughters you left behind will fall by the sword.'

**v22** Then you will do as I have done: You will not cover your lips or eat the bread of mourners.
**v23** Your turbans will remain on your heads and your sandals on your feet. You will not mourn or weep, but you will waste away because of your sins, and you will groan among yourselves.

**v24** 'Thus Ezekiel will be a sign for you; you will do everything that he has done. When this happens, you will know that I am the Lord GOD.'

**v25** And you, son of man, know that on the day I take away their stronghold, their pride and joy—the desire of their eyes which uplifted their souls—and their sons and daughters as well,
**v26** on that day a fugitive will come and tell you the news.
**v27** On that day your mouth will be opened to him who has escaped; you will speak and no longer be mute. So you will be a sign to them, and they will know that I am the LORD."
[^1]: Or let no lot fall upon it ( 24:6)

### Chapter 25

#### A Prophecy against Ammon
**v1** Then the word of the LORD came to me, saying,
**v2** "Son of man, set your face against the Ammonites and prophesy against them.
**v3** Tell the Ammonites to hear the word of the Lord GOD, for this is what the Lord GOD says: 'Because you exclaimed, "Aha!" when My sanctuary was profaned, when the land of Israel was laid waste, and when the house of Judah went into exile,
**v4** therefore I will indeed give you as a possession to the people of the East. They will set up their camps and pitch their tents among you. They will eat your fruit and drink your milk.
**v5** I will make Rabbah a pasture for camels, and Ammon [^1] a resting place for sheep. Then you will know that I am the LORD.'

**v6** For this is what the Lord GOD says: 'Because you clapped your hands and stomped your feet and rejoiced over the land of Israel with a heart full of contempt,
**v7** therefore I will indeed stretch out My hand against you and give you as plunder to the nations. I will cut you off from the peoples and exterminate you from the countries. I will destroy you, and you will know that I am the LORD.'
#### A Prophecy against Moab

**v8** This is what the Lord GOD says: 'Because Moab and Seir [^2] said, "Look, the house of Judah is like all the other nations,"
**v9** therefore I will indeed expose the flank of Moab beginning with its frontier cities—Beth-jeshimoth, Baal-meon, and Kiriathaim—the glory of the land.
**v10** I will give it along with the Ammonites as a possession to the people of the East, so that the Ammonites will no longer be remembered among the nations.
**v11** So I will execute judgments on Moab, and they will know that I am the LORD.'
#### A Prophecy against Edom

**v12** This is what the Lord GOD says: 'Because Edom acted vengefully against the house of Judah, and in so doing incurred grievous guilt,
**v13** therefore this is what the Lord GOD says: I will stretch out My hand against Edom and cut off from it both man and beast. I will make it a wasteland, and from Teman to Dedan they will fall by the sword.
**v14** I will take My vengeance on Edom by the hand of My people Israel, and they will deal with Edom according to My anger and wrath. Then they will know My vengeance, declares the Lord GOD.'
#### A Prophecy against the Philistines

**v15** This is what the Lord GOD says: 'Because the Philistines acted in vengeance, taking vengeance with malice of soul to destroy Judah with ancient hostility,
**v16** therefore this is what the Lord GOD says: Behold, I will stretch out My hand against the Philistines, and I will cut off the Cherethites and destroy the remnant along the coast.
**v17** I will execute great vengeance against them with furious reproof. Then they will know that I am the LORD, when I lay My vengeance upon them.'"
[^1]: Hebrew and the Ammonites ( 25:5)
[^2]: LXX does not include and Seir. ( 25:8)

### Chapter 26

#### A Prophecy against Tyre
**v1** In the eleventh month of the twelfth year, [^1] on the first day of the month, the word of the LORD came to me, saying,
**v2** "Son of man, because Tyre has said of Jerusalem, 'Aha! The gate to the nations is broken; it has swung open to me; now that she lies in ruins I will be filled,'
**v3** therefore this is what the Lord GOD says: 'Behold, O Tyre, I am against you, and I will raise up many nations against you, as the sea brings up its waves.
**v4** They will destroy the walls of Tyre and demolish her towers. I will scrape the soil from her and make her a bare rock.
**v5** She will become a place to spread nets in the sea, for I have spoken, declares the Lord GOD. She will become plunder for the nations,
**v6** and the villages on her mainland will be slain by the sword. Then they will know that I am the LORD.'

**v7** For this is what the Lord GOD says: 'Behold, I will bring against Tyre from the north Nebuchadnezzar [^2] king of Babylon, king of kings, with horses and chariots, with cavalry and a great company of troops.
**v8** He will slaughter the villages of your mainland with the sword; he will set up siege works against you, build a ramp to your walls, and raise his shields against you.
**v9** He will direct the blows of his battering rams against your walls and tear down your towers with his axes.
**v10** His multitude of horses will cover you in their dust.When he enters your gates as an army entering a breached city, your walls will shake from the noise of cavalry, wagons, and chariots.
**v11** The hooves of his horses will trample all your streets. He will slaughter your people with the sword, and your mighty pillars will fall to the ground.
**v12** They will plunder your wealth and pillage your merchandise. They will demolish your walls, tear down your beautiful homes, and throw your stones and timber and soil into the water.

**v13** So I will silence the sound of your songs, and the music of your lyres will no longer be heard.
**v14** I will make you a bare rock, and you will become a place to spread the fishing nets. You will never be rebuilt, for I, the LORD, have spoken, declares the Lord GOD.'

**v15** This is what the Lord GOD says to Tyre: 'Will not the coastlands quake at the sound of your downfall, when the wounded groan at the slaughter in your midst?

**v16** All the princes of the sea will descend from their thrones, remove their robes, and strip off their embroidered garments. Clothed with terror, they will sit on the ground, trembling every moment, appalled over you.
**v17** Then they will lament for you, saying,"How you have perished, O city of renowninhabited by seafaring men—she who was powerful on the sea, along with her people, who imposed terror on all peoples! [^3]
**v18** Now the coastlands trembleon the day of your downfall; the islands in the seaare dismayed by your demise."'

**v19** For this is what the Lord GOD says: 'When I make you a desolate city like other deserted cities, and when I raise up the deep against you so that the mighty waters cover you,
**v20** then I will bring you down with those who descend to the Pit, to the people of antiquity. I will make you dwell in the earth below like the ancient ruins, with those who descend to the Pit, so that you will no longer be inhabited or set in splendor [^4] in the land of the living.
**v21** I will make you an object of horror, and you will be no more. You will be sought, but will never be found,' declares the Lord GOD."
[^1]: Likely reading of the original Hebrew text; MT In the eleventh year ( 26:1)
[^2]: Hebrew Nebuchadrezzar, a variant of Nebuchadnezzar (king of Babylon). The latter spelling is used throughout Ezekiel for consistency. ( 26:7)
[^3]: Or on all her inhabitants ( 26:17)
[^4]: LXX or take your place ( 26:20)

### Chapter 27

#### A Lament for Tyre
**v1** Then the word of the LORD came to me, saying,
**v2** "Now you, son of man, take up a lament for Tyre.
**v3** Tell Tyre, who dwells at the gateway to the sea, merchant of the peoples on many coasts, that this is what the Lord GOD says:You have said, O Tyre,'I am perfect in beauty.'
**v4** Your borders are in the heart of the seas; your builders perfected your beauty.
**v5** They constructed all your plankingwith cypress [^1] from Senir. [^2] They took a cedar from Lebanonto make a mast for you.
**v6** Of oaks from Bashanthey made your oars; of wood from the coasts of Cyprus [^3] they made your deck, inlaid with ivory.
**v7** Of embroidered fine linen from Egyptthey made your sail, which served as your banner.Of blue and purple from the coasts of Elishahthey made your awning.

**v8** The men of Sidon and Arvadwere your oarsmen.Your men of skill, O Tyre, were there as your captains.
**v9** The elders of Gebal were aboard as shipwrights, repairing your leaks.All the ships of the sea and their sailorscame alongside to barter for your merchandise.

**v10** Men of Persia, Lydia, and Putserved as warriors in your army.They hung their shields and helmets on your walls; they gave you splendor.
**v11** Men of Arvad and Helechmanned your walls all around, and the men of Gammadwere in your towers.They hung their shields around your walls; they perfected your beauty.

**v12** Tarshish was your merchant because of your great wealth of goods; they exchanged silver, iron, tin, and lead for your wares.

**v13** Javan, [^4] Tubal, and Meshech were your merchants. They exchanged slaves and bronze utensils for your merchandise.

**v14** The men of Beth-togarmah exchanged horses, war horses, and mules for your wares.

**v15** The men of Dedan [^5] were your clients; many coastlands were your market; they paid you with ivory tusks and ebony.

**v16** Aram [^6] was your customer because of your many products; they exchanged turquoise, purple, embroidered work, fine linen, coral, and rubies for your wares.

**v17** Judah and the land of Israel traded with you; they exchanged wheat from Minnith, cakes and honey, oil and balm for your merchandise.

**v18** Because of your many products and your great wealth of goods, Damascus traded with you wine from Helbon, wool from Zahar,
**v19** and casks of wine from Izal for your wares. [^7] Wrought iron, cassia, and sweet cane [^8] were exchanged for your merchandise. [^9]

**v20** Dedan was your merchant in saddlecloths for riding.

**v21** Arabia and all the princes of Kedar were your customers, trading in lambs, rams, and goats.

**v22** The merchants of Sheba and Raamah traded with you; for your wares they exchanged gold, the finest of all spices, and precious stones.

**v23** Haran, Canneh, and Eden traded with you, and so did the merchants of Sheba, Asshur, and Chilmad.
**v24** In your marketplace they traded with you fine garments of blue, embroidered work, and multicolored rugs with cords tightly twisted and knotted.

**v25** The ships of Tarshish [^10] carried your merchandise.And you were filled with heavy cargoin the heart of the sea.
**v26** Your oarsmen have brought youonto the high seas, but the east wind will shatter youin the heart of the sea.
**v27** Your wealth, wares, and merchandise, your sailors, captains, and shipwrights, your merchants and all the warriors within you, with all the other people on board, will sink into the heart of the seaon the day of your downfall.

**v28** The countryside will shakewhen your sailors cry out.
**v29** All who handle the oarswill abandon their ships.The sailors and all the captains of the seawill stand on the shore.
**v30** They will raise their voices for you and cry out bitterly.They will throw dust on their headsand roll in ashes.
**v31** They will shave their heads for you and wrap themselves in sackcloth.They will weep over youwith anguish of soul and bitter mourning.

**v32** As they wail and mourn over you, they will take up a lament for you: 'Who was ever like Tyre, silenced in the middle of the sea?
**v33** When your wares went out to sea, you satisfied many nations.You enriched the kings of the earthwith your abundant wealth and merchandise.
**v34** Now you are shattered by the seasin the depths of the waters; your merchandise and the people among youhave gone down with you.
**v35** All the people of the coastlandsare appalled over you.Their kings shudder with fear; their faces are contorted.
**v36** Those who trade among the nationshiss at you; you have come to a horrible endand will be no more.'"
[^1]: Or pine or juniper or fir ( 27:5)
[^2]: That is, Mount Hermon ( 27:5)
[^3]: Hebrew Kittim ( 27:6)
[^4]: That is, Greece ( 27:13)
[^5]: Hebrew; LXX Rhodes ( 27:15)
[^6]: Most Hebrew manuscripts; some Hebrew manuscripts and Syriac Edom ( 27:16)
[^7]: Probable reading; MT—and Dan and Javan from Uzal (traded) for your wares ( 27:19)
[^8]: Or calamus ( 27:19)
[^9]: Or were among your merchandise ( 27:19)
[^10]: Or A fleet of trading ships ( 27:25)

### Chapter 28

#### A Prophecy against the Ruler of Tyre
**v1** And the word of the LORD came to me, saying,
**v2** "Son of man, tell the ruler of Tyre that this is what the Lord GOD says:Your heart is proud, and you have said,'I am a god; I sit in the seat of godsin the heart of the sea.' Yet you are a man and not a god, though you have regarded your heartas that of a god.

**v3** Behold, you are wiser than Daniel; no secret is hidden from you!
**v4** By your wisdom and understandingyou have gained your wealthand amassed gold and silverfor your treasuries.
**v5** By your great skill in tradingyou have increased your wealth, but your heart has grown proudbecause of it.

**v6** Therefore this is what the Lord GOD says:Because you regard your heartas the heart of a god,
**v7** behold, I will bring foreigners against you, the most ruthless of nations.They will draw their swordsagainst the beauty of your wisdomand will defile your splendor.
**v8** They will bring you down to the Pit, and you will die a violent deathin the heart of the seas.

**v9** Will you still say, 'I am a god,'in the presence of those who slay you?You will be only a man, not a god, in the hands of those who wound you.
**v10** You will die the death of the uncircumcisedat the hands of foreigners.For I have spoken, declares the Lord GOD."
#### A Lament for the King of Tyre

**v11** Again the word of the LORD came to me, saying,
**v12** "Son of man, take up a lament for the king of Tyre and tell him that this is what the Lord GOD says: 'You were the seal of perfection, full of wisdom and perfect in beauty.
**v13** You were in Eden, the garden of God.Every kind of precious stone adorned you: [^1] ruby, topaz, and diamond, beryl, onyx, and jasper, sapphire, [^2] turquoise, and emerald.Your mountings and settings were crafted in gold, prepared on the day of your creation.

**v14** You were anointed as a guardian cherub, for I had ordained you.You were on the holy mountain of God; you walked among the fiery stones.
**v15** From the day you were createdyou were blameless in your ways—until wickedness was found in you.

**v16** By the vastness of your trade, you were filled with violence, and you sinned.So I drove you in disgracefrom the mountain of God, and I banished you, O guardian cherub, from among the fiery stones.
**v17** Your heart grew proud of your beauty; you corrupted your wisdom because of your splendor; so I cast you to the earth; I made you a spectacle before kings.

**v18** By the multitude of your iniquitiesand the dishonesty of your tradingyou have profaned your sanctuaries.So I made fire come from within you, and it consumed you.I reduced you to ashes on the groundin the eyes of all who saw you.
**v19** All the nations who know youare appalled over you.You have come to a horrible endand will be no more.'"
#### A Prophecy against Sidon

**v20** Then the word of the LORD came to me, saying,
**v21** "Son of man, set your face against Sidon and prophesy against her.
**v22** And you are to declare that this is what the Lord GOD says: 'Behold, I am against you, O Sidon, and I will be glorified within you.They will know that I am the LORDwhen I execute judgments against herand demonstrate My holiness through her.
**v23** I will send a plague against herand shed blood in her streets; the slain will fall within her, while the sword is against her on every side.Then they will know that I am the LORD.

**v24** For the people of Israel will no longer face a pricking brier or a painful thorn from all around them who treat them with contempt. Then they will know that I am the Lord GOD.'
#### The Restoration of Israel

**v25** This is what the Lord GOD says: 'When I gather the house of Israel from the peoples among whom they have been scattered, I will show Myself holy among them in the sight of the nations.Then they will dwell in their own land, which I have given to My servant Jacob.
**v26** And there they will dwell securely, build houses, and plant vineyards. They will dwell securely when I execute judgments against all those around them who treat them with contempt. Then they will know that I am the LORD their God.'"
[^1]: The precise identification of some of these gemstones is uncertain. ( 28:13)
[^2]: Or lapis lazuli ( 28:13)

### Chapter 29

#### A Prophecy against Pharaoh
**v1** In the tenth year, on the twelfth day of the tenth month, the word of the LORD came to me, saying,
**v2** "Son of man, set your face against Pharaoh king of Egypt and prophesy against him and against all Egypt.
**v3** Speak to him and tell him that this is what the Lord GOD says:Behold, I am against you, O Pharaoh king of Egypt, O great monster who liesamong his rivers, who says, 'The Nile is mine; I made it myself.'

**v4** But I will put hooks in your jawsand cause the fish of your streamsto cling to your scales.I will haul you up out of your rivers, and all the fish of your streamswill cling to your scales.
**v5** I will leave you in the desert, you and all the fish of your streams.You will fall on the open fieldand will not be taken awayor gathered for burial.I have given you as foodto the beasts of the earthand the birds of the air.
**v6** Then all the people of Egyptwill know that I am the LORD. For you were only a staff of reedsto the house of Israel.
**v7** When Israel took hold of you with their hands, you splintered, tearing all their shoulders; when they leaned on you, you broke, and their backs were wrenched. [^1]
#### The Desolation of Egypt

**v8** Therefore this is what the Lord GOD says: I will bring a sword against you and cut off from you man and beast.
**v9** The land of Egypt will become a desolate wasteland. Then they will know that I am the LORD.Because you said, 'The Nile is mine; I made it,'
**v10** therefore I am against you and against your rivers. I will turn the land of Egypt into a ruin, a desolate wasteland from Migdol to Syene, and as far as the border of Cush. [^2]
**v11** No foot of man or beast will pass through, and it will be uninhabited for forty years.

**v12** I will make the land of Egypt a desolation among desolate lands, and her cities will lie desolate for forty years among the ruined cities. And I will disperse the Egyptians among the nations and scatter them throughout the countries.

**v13** For this is what the Lord GOD says: At the end of forty years I will gather the Egyptians from the nations to which they were scattered.
**v14** I will restore Egypt from captivity [^3] and bring them back to the land of Pathros, the land of their origin. There they will be a lowly kingdom.

**v15** Egypt will be the lowliest of kingdoms and will never again exalt itself above the nations. For I will diminish Egypt so that it will never again rule over the nations.
**v16** Egypt will never again be an object of trust for the house of Israel, but will remind them of their iniquity in turning to the Egyptians. Then they will know that I am the Lord GOD."
#### Egypt the Reward of Nebuchadnezzar

**v17** In the twenty-seventh year, on the first day of the first month, the word of the LORD came to me, saying,
**v18** "Son of man, Nebuchadnezzar king of Babylon caused his army to labor strenuously against Tyre. Every head was made bald and every shoulder made raw. But he and his army received no wages from Tyre for the labor they expended on it.

**v19** Therefore this is what the Lord GOD says: I will give the land of Egypt to Nebuchadnezzar king of Babylon, who will carry off its wealth, seize its spoil, and remove its plunder. This will be the wages for his army.
**v20** I have given him the land of Egypt as the reward for his labor, because it was done for Me, declares the Lord GOD.

**v21** In that day I will cause a horn to sprout for the house of Israel, and I will open your mouth to speak among them. Then they will know that I am the LORD."
[^1]: Syriac (see also LXX and Vulgate); Hebrew and you caused their loins to shake. ( 29:7)
[^2]: That is, the upper Nile region ( 29:10)
[^3]: Or restore the fortunes of Egypt ( 29:14)

### Chapter 30

#### A Lament for Egypt
**v1** Again the word of the LORD came to me, saying,
**v2** "Son of man, prophesy and declare that this is what the Lord GOD says:Wail, 'Alasfor that day!'
**v3** For the day is near, the Day of the LORD is near.It will be a day of clouds, a time of doom for the nations. [^1]

**v4** A sword will come against Egypt, and there will be anguish in Cush [^2] when the slain fall in Egypt, its wealth is taken away, and its foundations are torn down.
**v5** Cush, Put, and Lud, [^3] and all the various peoples, as well as Libya and the men of the covenant land, will fall with Egypt by the sword.

**v6** For this is what the LORD says:The allies of Egypt will fall, and her proud strength will collapse.From Migdol to Syene [^4] they will fall by the sword within her, declares the Lord GOD.
**v7** They will be desolate among desolate lands, and their cities will lie among ruined cities.

**v8** Then they will know that I am the LORDwhen I set fire to Egyptand all her helpers are shattered.

**v9** On that day messengers will go out from Me in ships to frighten Cush out of complacency. Anguish will come upon them on the day of Egypt's doom. [^5] For it is indeed coming.

**v10** This is what the Lord GOD says:I will put an end to the hordes of Egyptby the hand of Nebuchadnezzar king of Babylon.
**v11** He and his people with him, the most ruthless of the nations, will be brought in to destroy the land.They will draw their swords against Egyptand fill the land with the slain.
**v12** I will make the streams dry upand sell the land to the wicked.By the hands of foreigners I will bring desolationupon the land and everything in it.I, the LORD, have spoken.

**v13** This is what the Lord GOD says:I will destroy the idolsand put an end to the images in Memphis. [^6] There will no longer be a prince in Egypt, and I will instill fear in that land.

**v14** I will lay waste Pathros, set fire to Zoan, and execute judgment on Thebes. [^7]
**v15** I will pour out My wrath on Pelusium, [^8] the stronghold of Egypt, and cut off the crowds of Thebes.
**v16** I will set fire to Egypt, Pelusium will writhe in anguish, Thebes will be split open, and Memphis will face daily distress.

**v17** The young men of On and Pi-beseth [^9] will fall by the sword, and those cities will go into captivity.
**v18** The day will be darkened in Tahpanheswhen I break the yoke of Egyptand her proud strength comes to an end.A cloud will cover her, and her daughters will go into captivity.

**v19** So I will execute judgment on Egypt, and they will know that I am the LORD."
#### Pharaoh's Power Broken

**v20** In the eleventh year, on the seventh day of the first month, the word of the LORD came to me, saying,
**v21** "Son of man, I have broken the arm of Pharaoh king of Egypt. See, it has not been bound up for healing, or splinted for strength to hold the sword.

**v22** Therefore this is what the Lord GOD says: Behold, I am against Pharaoh king of Egypt. I will break his arms, both the strong one and the one already broken, and will make the sword fall from his hand.
**v23** I will disperse the Egyptians among the nations and scatter them throughout the lands.

**v24** I will strengthen the arms of Babylon's king and place My sword in his hand, but I will break the arms of Pharaoh, who will groan before him like a mortally wounded man.
**v25** I will strengthen the arms of Babylon's king, but Pharaoh's arms will fall limp.Then they will know that I am the LORD, when I place My sword in the hand of Babylon's king, and he wields it against the land of Egypt.
**v26** I will disperse the Egyptians among the nations and scatter them throughout the lands. Then they will know that I am the LORD."
[^1]: Hebrew does not include of doom. ( 30:3)
[^2]: That is, the upper Nile region; also in verses 5 and 9 ( 30:4)
[^3]: Or Lydia ( 30:5)
[^4]: That is, Aswan; see Isaiah 49:12 ( 30:6)
[^5]: Hebrew the day of Egypt ( 30:9)
[^6]: LXX; Hebrew Noph; also in verse 16 ( 30:13)
[^7]: Hebrew No; also in verses 15 and 16 ( 30:14)
[^8]: Hebrew Sin; also in verse 16 ( 30:15)
[^9]: That is, Heliopolis and Bubastis, as in LXX; Hebrew Aven and Pi-beseth ( 30:17)

### Chapter 31

#### Egypt Will Fall like Assyria
**v1** In the eleventh year, on the first day of the third month, the word of the LORD came to me, saying,
**v2** "Son of man, say to Pharaoh king of Egypt and to his multitude: 'Who can be comparedto your greatness?
**v3** Look at Assyria, a cedar in Lebanon, with beautiful branches that shaded the forest.It towered on high; its top was among the clouds.
**v4** The waters made it grow; the deep springs made it tall, directing their streams all around its baseand sending their channels to all the trees of the field.

**v5** Therefore it towered higherthan all the trees of the field.Its branches multiplied, and its boughs grew longas it spread them outbecause of the abundant waters.
**v6** All the birds of the airnested in its branches, and all the beasts of the fieldgave birth beneath its boughs; all the great nationslived in its shade.

**v7** It was beautiful in its greatness, in the length of its limbs, for its roots extendedto abundant waters.
**v8** The cedars in the garden of Godcould not rival it; the cypresses [^1] could not compare with its branches, nor the plane trees [^2] match its boughs.No tree in the garden of Godcould compare with its beauty.
**v9** I made it beautiful with its many branches, the envy of all the trees of Eden, which were in the garden of God.'

**v10** Therefore this is what the Lord GOD says: 'Since it became great [^3] in height and set its top among the clouds, [^4] and it grew proud on account of its height,
**v11** I delivered it into the hand of the ruler of the nations, for him to deal with it according to its wickedness. I have banished it.

**v12** Foreigners, the most ruthless of the nations, cut it down and left it. Its branches have fallen on the mountains and in every valley; its boughs lay broken in all the earth's ravines. And all the peoples of the earth left its shade and abandoned it.

**v13** All the birds of the air nested on its fallen trunk, and all the beasts of the field lived among its boughs.
**v14** This happened so that no other trees by the waters would become great in height and set their tops among the clouds, and no other well-watered trees would reach them in height. For they have all been consigned to death, to the depths of the earth, among the mortals who descend to the Pit.'

**v15** This is what the Lord GOD says: 'On the day it was brought down to Sheol, I caused mourning. I covered the deep because of it; I held back its rivers; its abundant waters were restrained. I made Lebanon mourn for it, and all the trees of the field fainted because of it.
**v16** I made the nations quake at the sound of its downfall, when I cast it down to Sheol with those who descend to the Pit.Then all the trees of Eden, the choicest and best of Lebanon, all the well-watered trees, were consoled in the earth below.
**v17** They too descended with it to Sheol, to those slain by the sword. As its allies they had lived in its shade among the nations.

**v18** Who then is like you in glory and greatness among the trees of Eden? You also will be brought down to the depths of the earth to be with the trees of Eden. You will lie among the uncircumcised, with those slain by the sword. This is Pharaoh and all his multitude, declares the Lord GOD.'"
[^1]: Or pines or junipers or firs ( 31:8)
[^2]: Possibly chestnut or juniper ( 31:8)
[^3]: Hebrew you became great ( 31:10)
[^4]: Or through the thick boughs ( 31:10)

### Chapter 32

#### A Lament for Pharaoh King of Egypt
**v1** In the twelfth year, on the first day of the twelfth month, the word of the LORD came to me, saying,
**v2** "Son of man, take up a lament for Pharaoh king of Egypt and say to him: 'You are like a lion among the nations; you are like a monster in the seas.You thrash about in your rivers, churning up the waters with your feetand muddying the streams.'

**v3** This is what the Lord GOD says: 'I will spread My net over youwith a company of many peoples, and they will draw you up in My net.
**v4** I will abandon you on the landand hurl you into the open field.I will cause all the birds of the airto settle upon you, and all the beasts of the earthto eat their fill of you.
**v5** I will put your flesh on the mountainsand fill the valleys with your remains. [^1]
**v6** I will drench the landwith the flow of your blood, all the way to the mountains—the ravines will be filled.

**v7** When I extinguish you, I will cover the heavensand darken their stars.I will cover the sun with a cloud, and the moon will not give its light.
**v8** All the shining lights in the heavens I will darken over you, and I will bring darknessupon your land,'declares the Lord GOD.
**v9** 'I will trouble the hearts of many peoples, when I bring about your destruction among the nations, in countries [^2] you do not know.
**v10** I will cause many peoplesto be appalled over you, and their kings will shudder in horror because of youwhen I brandish My sword before them.On the day of your downfalleach of them will trembleevery moment for his life.'

**v11** For this is what the Lord GOD says: 'The sword of the king of Babylonwill come against you!
**v12** I will make your hordes fallby the swords of the mighty, the most ruthless of all nations.They will ravage the pride of Egyptand all her multitudes will be destroyed.
**v13** I will slaughter all her cattlebeside the abundant waters.No human foot will muddy them again, and no cattle hooves will disturb them.
**v14** Then I will let her waters settleand will make her rivers flow like oil,'declares the Lord GOD.
**v15** 'When I make the land of Egypt a desolationand empty it of all that filled it, when I strike down all who live there, then they will know that I am the LORD.'
**v16** This is the lament they will chant for her; the daughters of the nations will chant it. Over Egypt and all her multitudes they will chant it, declares the Lord GOD."
#### Egypt Cast into the Pit

**v17** In the twelfth year, on the fifteenth day of the month, [^3] the word of the LORD came to me, saying,
**v18** "Son of man, wail for the multitudes of Egypt, and consign her and the daughters of the mighty nations to the depths of the earth with those who descend to the Pit:

**v19** Whom do you surpass in beauty?Go down and be placed with the uncircumcised!
**v20** They will fall among those slain by the sword.The sword is appointed!Let them drag her awayalong with all her multitudes.

**v21** Mighty chiefs will speak from the midst of Sheolabout Egypt and her allies: 'They have come down and lie with the uncircumcised, with those slain by the sword.'

**v22** Assyria is there with her whole company; her graves are all around her.All of them are slain, fallen by the sword.
**v23** Her graves are set in the depths of the Pit, and her company is all around her grave.All of them are slain, fallen by the sword—those who once spread terrorin the land of the living.

**v24** Elam is therewith all her multitudes around her grave.All of them are slain, fallen by the sword—those who went down uncircumcisedto the earth below, who once spread their terrorin the land of the living.They bear their disgracewith those who descend to the Pit.
**v25** Among the slain they preparea resting place for Elamwith all her hordes, with her graves all around her.All of them are uncircumcised, slain by the sword, although their terror was once spreadin the land of the living.They bear their disgracewith those who descend to the Pit.They are placed among the slain.

**v26** Meshech and Tubal are therewith all their multitudes, with their graves all around them.All of them are uncircumcised, slain by the sword, because they spread their terrorin the land of the living.
**v27** They do not lie downwith the fallen warriors of old, [^4] who went down to Sheolwith their weapons of war, whose swords were placed under their heads, whose shields [^5] rested on their bones, although the terror of the mightywas once in the land of the living.
**v28** But you too will be shatteredand lie down among the uncircumcised, with those slain by the sword.

**v29** Edom is there, and all her kings and princes, who despite their mightare laid among those slain by the sword.They lie down with the uncircumcised, with those who descend to the Pit.

**v30** All the leaders of the northand all the Sidonians are there; they went down in disgrace with the slain, despite the terror of their might.They lie uncircumcisedwith those slain by the swordand bear their shamewith those who descend to the Pit.

**v31** Pharaoh will see themand be comforted over all his multitude—Pharaoh and all his army, slain by the sword, declares the Lord GOD.
**v32** For I will spread My terrorin the land of the living, so that Pharaoh and all his multitudewill be laid to rest among the uncircumcised, with those slain by the sword, declares the Lord GOD."
[^1]: Or your lofty stature ( 32:5)
[^2]: Hebrew; LXX when I lead you into captivity among the nations, into countries ( 32:9)
[^3]: Presumably the fifteenth day of the twelfth month (see verse 1); LXX on the fifteenth day of the first month. ( 32:17)
[^4]: LXX; Hebrew warriors of the uncircumcised ( 32:27)
[^5]: Likely reading of the original Hebrew text; MT iniquities ( 32:27)

### Chapter 33

#### Ezekiel the Watchman for Israel
**v1** Again the word of the LORD came to me, saying,
**v2** "Son of man, speak to your people and tell them: 'Suppose I bring the sword against a land, and the people of that land choose a man from among them, appointing him as their watchman,
**v3** and he sees the sword coming against that land and blows the ram's horn to warn the people.

**v4** Then if anyone hears the sound of the horn but fails to heed the warning, and the sword comes and takes him away, his blood will be on his own head.
**v5** Since he heard the sound of the horn but failed to heed the warning, his blood will be on his own head. If he had heeded the warning, he would have saved his life.

**v6** But if the watchman sees the sword coming and fails to blow the horn to warn the people, and the sword comes and takes away a life, then that one will be taken away in his iniquity, but I will hold the watchman accountable for his blood.'

**v7** As for you, O son of man, I have made you a watchman for the house of Israel; so hear the word from My mouth and give them the warning from Me.
**v8** If I say to the wicked, 'O wicked man, you will surely die,' but you do not speak out to dissuade him from his way, then that wicked man will die in his iniquity, yet I will hold you accountable for his blood.
**v9** But if you warn the wicked man to turn from his way, and he does not turn from it, he will die in his iniquity, but you will have saved your life. [^1]
#### The Message of the Watchman

**v10** Now as for you, son of man, tell the house of Israel that this is what they have said: 'Our transgressions and our sins are heavy upon us, and we are wasting away because of them! How can we live?'

**v11** Say to them: 'As surely as I live, declares the Lord GOD, I take no pleasure in the death of the wicked, but rather that the wicked should turn from their ways and live. Turn! Turn from your evil ways! For why should you die, O house of Israel?'

**v12** Therefore, son of man, say to your people: 'The righteousness of the righteous man will not deliver him in the day of his transgression; neither will the wickedness of the wicked man cause him to stumble on the day he turns from his wickedness. Nor will the righteous man be able to survive by his righteousness on the day he sins.'

**v13** If I tell the righteous man that he will surely live, but he then trusts in his righteousness and commits iniquity, then none of his righteous works will be remembered; he will die because of the iniquity he has committed.

**v14** But if I tell the wicked man, 'You will surely die,' and he turns from his sin and does what is just and right—
**v15** if he restores a pledge, makes restitution for what he has stolen, and walks in the statutes of life without practicing iniquity—then he will surely live; he will not die.
**v16** None of the sins he has committed will be held against him. He has done what is just and right; he will surely live.

**v17** Yet your people say, 'The way of the Lord is not just.' But it is their way that is not just.
**v18** If a righteous man turns from his righteousness and commits iniquity, he will die for it.
**v19** But if a wicked man turns from his wickedness and does what is just and right, he will live because of this.

**v20** Yet you say, 'The way of the Lord is not just.' But I will judge each of you according to his ways, O house of Israel."
#### Word of Jerusalem's Fall

**v21** In the twelfth year of our exile, on the fifth day of the tenth month, a fugitive from Jerusalem came to me and reported, "The city has been taken!"

**v22** Now the evening before the fugitive arrived, the hand of the LORD was upon me, and He opened my mouth before the man came to me in the morning. So my mouth was opened and I was no longer mute.

**v23** Then the word of the LORD came to me, saying,
**v24** "Son of man, those living in the ruins in the land of Israel are saying, 'Abraham was only one man, yet he possessed the land. But we are many; surely the land has been given to us as a possession.'

**v25** Therefore tell them that this is what the Lord GOD says: 'You eat meat with the blood in it, lift up your eyes to your idols, and shed blood. Should you then possess the land?
**v26** You have relied on your swords, you have committed detestable acts, and each of you has defiled his neighbor's wife. Should you then possess the land?'

**v27** Tell them that this is what the Lord GOD says: 'As surely as I live, those in the ruins will fall by the sword, those in the open field I will give to be devoured by wild animals, and those in the strongholds and caves will die by plague.
**v28** I will make the land a desolate waste, and the pride of her strength will come to an end. The mountains of Israel will become desolate, so that no one will pass through.
**v29** Then they will know that I am the LORD, when I have made the land a desolate waste because of all the abominations they have committed.'

**v30** As for you, son of man, your people are talking about you near the city walls and in the doorways of their houses. One speaks to another, each saying to his brother, 'Come and hear the message that has come from the LORD!'

**v31** So My people come to you as usual, sit before you, and hear your words; but they do not put them into practice. Although they express love with their mouths, their hearts pursue dishonest gain.
**v32** Indeed, you are to them like a singer of love songs with a beautiful voice, who skillfully plays an instrument. They hear your words but do not put them into practice.
**v33** So when it comes to pass—and surely it will come—then they will know that a prophet has been among them."
[^1]: See Acts 20:25–26 ( 33:9)

### Chapter 34

#### A Prophecy against Israel's Shepherds
**v1** Then the word of the LORD came to me, saying,
**v2** "Son of man, prophesy against the shepherds of Israel. Prophesy and tell them that this is what the Lord GOD says: 'Woe to the shepherds of Israel, who only feed themselves! Should not the shepherds feed their flock?
**v3** You eat the fat, wear the wool, and butcher the fattened sheep, but you do not feed the flock.

**v4** You have not strengthened the weak, healed the sick, bound up the injured, brought back the strays, or searched for the lost. Instead, you have ruled them with violence and cruelty.
**v5** They were scattered for lack of a shepherd, and when they were scattered they became food for all the wild beasts.
**v6** My flock went astray on all the mountains and every high hill. They were scattered over the face of all the earth, with no one to search for them or seek them out.'

**v7** Therefore, you shepherds, hear the word of the LORD:
**v8** 'As surely as I live, declares the Lord GOD, because My flock lacks a shepherd and has become prey and food for every wild beast, and because My shepherds did not search for My flock but fed themselves instead,
**v9** therefore, you shepherds, hear the word of the LORD!'

**v10** This is what the Lord GOD says: 'Behold, I am against the shepherds, and I will demand from them My flock and remove them from tending the flock, so that they can no longer feed themselves. For I will deliver My flock from their mouths, and it will no longer be food for them.'
#### The Good Shepherd

**v11** For this is what the Lord GOD says: 'Behold, I Myself will search for My flock and seek them out.
**v12** As a shepherd looks for his scattered sheep when he is among the flock, so I will look for My flock.I will rescue them from all the places to which they were scattered on a day of clouds and darkness.
**v13** I will bring them out from the peoples, gather them from the countries, and bring them into their own land. I will feed them on the mountains of Israel, in the ravines, and in all the settlements of the land.
**v14** I will feed them in good pasture, and the lofty mountains of Israel will be their grazing land. There they will lie down in a good grazing land; they will feed in rich pasture on the mountains of Israel.

**v15** I will tend My flock and make them lie down, declares the Lord GOD.
**v16** I will seek the lost, bring back the strays, bind up the broken, and strengthen the weak; but the sleek and strong I will destroy. I will shepherd them with justice.'

**v17** This is what the Lord GOD says to you, My flock: 'I will judge between one sheep and another, between the rams and the goats.
**v18** Is it not enough for you to feed on the good pasture? Must you also trample the rest of the pasture with your feet? Is it not enough for you to drink the clear waters? Must you also muddy the rest with your feet?
**v19** Why must My flock feed on what your feet have trampled, and drink what your feet have muddied?'

**v20** Therefore this is what the Lord GOD says to them: 'Behold, I Myself will judge between the fat sheep and the lean sheep.
**v21** Since you shove with flank and shoulder, butting all the weak ones with your horns until you have scattered them abroad,
**v22** I will save My flock, and they will no longer be prey. I will judge between one sheep and another.
**v23** I will appoint over them one shepherd, My servant David, and he will feed them. He will feed them and be their shepherd.
**v24** I, the LORD, will be their God, and My servant David will be a prince among them. I, the LORD, have spoken.
#### The Covenant of Peace

**v25** I will make with them a covenant of peace and rid the land of wild animals, so that they may dwell securely in the wilderness and sleep in the forest.
**v26** I will make them and the places around My hill a blessing. I will send down showers in season—showers of blessing.
**v27** The trees of the field will give their fruit, and the land will yield its produce; My flock will be secure in their land. Then they will know that I am the LORD, when I have broken the bars of their yoke and delivered them from the hands that enslaved them.

**v28** They will no longer be prey for the nations, and the beasts of the earth will not consume them. They will dwell securely, and no one will frighten them.

**v29** And I will raise up for them a garden of renown, and they will no longer be victims of famine in the land or bear the scorn of the nations.
**v30** Then they will know that I, the LORD their God, am with them, and that they, the house of Israel, are My people,' declares the Lord GOD.

**v31** 'You are My flock, the sheep of My pasture, My people, and I am your God,' declares the Lord GOD."
### Chapter 35

#### A Prophecy against Mount Seir
**v1** Moreover, the word of the LORD came to me, saying,
**v2** "Son of man, set your face against Mount Seir and prophesy against it,
**v3** and declare that this is what the Lord GOD says:Behold, I am against you, O Mount Seir.I will stretch out My hand against you and make you a desolate waste.
**v4** I will turn your cities into ruins, and you will become a desolation.Then you will know that I am the LORD.

**v5** Because you harbored an ancient hatred and delivered the Israelites over to the sword in the time of their disaster at the final stage of their punishment,
**v6** therefore as surely as I live, declares the Lord GOD, I will give you over to bloodshed and it will pursue you. Since you did not hate bloodshed, it will pursue you.

**v7** I will make Mount Seir a desolate waste and will cut off from it those who come and go.
**v8** I will fill its mountains with the slain; those killed by the sword will fall on your hills, in your valleys, and in all your ravines.
**v9** I will make you a perpetual desolation, and your cities will not be inhabited. Then you will know that I am the LORD.

**v10** Because you have said, 'These two nations and countries will be ours, and we will possess them,' even though the LORD was there,
**v11** therefore as surely as I live, declares the Lord GOD, I will treat you according to the anger and jealousy you showed in your hatred against them, and I will make Myself known among them when I judge you.

**v12** Then you will know that I, the LORD, have heard every contemptuous word you uttered against the mountains of Israel when you said, 'They are desolate; they are given to us to devour!'
**v13** You boasted against Me with your mouth and multiplied your words against Me. I heard it Myself!

**v14** This is what the Lord GOD says: While the whole earth rejoices, I will make you desolate.
**v15** As you rejoiced when the inheritance of the house of Israel became desolate, so will I do to you. You will become a desolation, O Mount Seir, and so will all of Edom. Then they will know that I am the LORD.
### Chapter 36

#### A Prophecy to the Mountains of Israel
**v1** "And you, son of man, prophesy to the mountains of Israel and say: O mountains of Israel, hear the word of the LORD.
**v2** This is what the Lord GOD says: Because the enemy has said of you, 'Aha! The ancient heights have become our possession,'
**v3** therefore prophesy and declare that this is what the Lord GOD says: Because they have made you desolate and have trampled you on every side, so that you became a possession of the rest of the nations and were taken up in slander by the lips of their talkers,
**v4** therefore, O mountains of Israel, hear the word of the Lord GOD.This is what the Lord GOD says to the mountains and hills, to the ravines and valleys, to the desolate ruins and abandoned cities, which have become a spoil and a mockery to the rest of the nations around you.
**v5** Therefore this is what the Lord GOD says: Surely in My burning zeal I have spoken against the rest of the nations, and against all Edom, who took My land as their own possession with wholehearted joy and utter contempt, so that its pastureland became plunder.

**v6** Therefore, prophesy concerning the land of Israel and tell the mountains and hills, the ravines and valleys, that this is what the Lord GOD says: Behold, I have spoken in My burning zeal because you have endured the reproach of the nations.

**v7** Therefore this is what the Lord GOD says: I have sworn with an uplifted hand that surely the nations around you will endure reproach of their own.
**v8** But you, O mountains of Israel, will produce branches and bear fruit for My people Israel, for they will soon come home.

**v9** For behold, I am on your side; I will turn toward you, and you will be tilled and sown.
**v10** I will multiply the people upon you—the house of Israel in its entirety. The cities will be inhabited and the ruins rebuilt.
**v11** I will fill you with people and animals, and they will multiply and be fruitful. I will make you as inhabited as you once were, and I will make you prosper more than before. Then you will know that I am the LORD.

**v12** Yes, I will cause My people Israel to walk upon you; they will possess you, and you will be their inheritance, and you will no longer deprive them of their children.

**v13** For this is what the Lord GOD says: Because people say to you, 'You devour men and deprive your nation of its children,'
**v14** therefore you will no longer devour men or deprive your nation of its children, declares the Lord GOD.
**v15** I will no longer allow the taunts of the nations to be heard against you, and you will no longer endure the reproach of the peoples or cause your nation to stumble, declares the Lord GOD."
#### A New Heart and a New Spirit

**v16** Again the word of the LORD came to me, saying,
**v17** "Son of man, when the people of Israel lived in their land, they defiled it by their own ways and deeds. Their behavior before Me was like the uncleanness of a woman's impurity.
**v18** So I poured out My wrath upon them because of the blood they had shed on the land, and because they had defiled it with their idols.

**v19** I dispersed them among the nations, and they were scattered throughout the lands. I judged them according to their ways and deeds.
**v20** And wherever they went among the nations, they profaned My holy name, because it was said of them, 'These are the people of the LORD, yet they had to leave His land.'
**v21** But I had concern for My holy name, which the house of Israel had profaned among the nations to which they had gone.

**v22** Therefore tell the house of Israel that this is what the Lord GOD says: It is not for your sake that I will act, O house of Israel, but for My holy name, which you profaned among the nations to which you went.
**v23** I will show the holiness of My great name, which has been profaned among the nations—the name you have profaned among them. Then the nations will know that I am the LORD, declares the Lord GOD, when I show My holiness in you before their eyes.

**v24** For I will take you from among the nations and gather you out of all the countries, and I will bring you back into your own land.
**v25** I will also sprinkle clean water on you, and you will be clean. I will cleanse you from all your impurities and all your idols.
**v26** I will give you a new heart and put a new spirit within you; I will remove your heart of stone and give you a heart of flesh.
**v27** And I will put My Spirit within you and cause you to walk in My statutes and to carefully observe My ordinances.

**v28** Then you will live in the land that I gave your forefathers; you will be My people, and I will be your God.
**v29** I will save you from all your uncleanness. I will summon the grain and make it plentiful, and I will not bring famine upon you.
**v30** I will also make the fruit of the trees and the crops of the field plentiful, so that you will no longer bear reproach among the nations on account of famine.

**v31** Then you will remember your evil ways and wicked deeds, and you will loathe yourselves for your iniquities and abominations.
**v32** It is not for your sake that I will act, declares the Lord GOD—let it be known to you. Be ashamed and disgraced for your ways, O house of Israel!

**v33** This is what the Lord GOD says: On the day I cleanse you from all your iniquities, I will cause the cities to be resettled and the ruins to be rebuilt.
**v34** The desolate land will be cultivated instead of lying desolate in the sight of all who pass through.
**v35** Then they will say, 'This land that was desolate has become like the garden of Eden. The cities that were once ruined, desolate, and destroyed are now fortified and inhabited.'

**v36** Then the nations around you that remain will know that I, the LORD, have rebuilt what was destroyed, and I have replanted what was desolate. I, the LORD, have spoken, and I will do it.

**v37** This is what the Lord GOD says: Once again I will hear the plea of the house of Israel and do for them this: I will multiply their people like a flock.
**v38** Like the numerous flocks for sacrifices at Jerusalem during her appointed feasts, so the ruined cities will be filled with flocks of people. Then they will know that I am the LORD."
### Chapter 37

#### The Valley of Dry Bones
**v1** The hand of the LORD was upon me, and He brought me out by His Spirit and set me down in the middle of the valley, and it was full of bones.
**v2** He led me all around among them, and I saw a great many bones on the floor of the valley, and indeed, they were very dry.

**v3** Then He asked me, "Son of man, can these bones come to life?""O Lord GOD," I replied, "only You know."

**v4** And He said to me, "Prophesy concerning these bones and tell them, 'Dry bones, hear the word of the LORD!
**v5** This is what the Lord GOD says to these bones: I will cause breath [^1] to enter you, and you will come to life.
**v6** I will attach tendons to you and make flesh grow upon you and cover you with skin. I will put breath within you so that you will come to life. Then you will know that I am the LORD.'"

**v7** So I prophesied as I had been commanded. And as I prophesied, there was suddenly a noise, a rattling, and the bones came together, bone to bone.
**v8** As I looked on, tendons appeared on them, flesh grew, and skin covered them; but there was no breath in them.

**v9** Then He said to me, "Prophesy to the breath; prophesy, son of man, and tell the breath that this is what the Lord GOD says: Come from the four winds, O breath, and breathe into these slain, so that they may live!"

**v10** So I prophesied as He had commanded me, and the breath entered them, and they came to life and stood on their feet—a vast army.

**v11** Then He said to me, "Son of man, these bones are the whole house of Israel. Look, they are saying, 'Our bones are dried up, and our hope has perished; we are cut off.'

**v12** Therefore prophesy and tell them that this is what the Lord GOD says: 'O My people, I will open your graves and bring you up from them, and I will bring you back to the land of Israel.
**v13** Then you, My people, will know that I am the LORD, when I open your graves and bring you up from them.
**v14** I will put My Spirit in you and you will live, and I will settle you in your own land. Then you will know that I, the LORD, have spoken, and I will do it, declares the LORD.'"
#### One Nation with One King

**v15** Again the word of the LORD came to me, saying,
**v16** "And you, son of man, take a single stick [^2] and write on it: 'Belonging to Judah and to the Israelites associated with him.' Then take another stick and write on it: 'Belonging to Joseph—the stick of Ephraim—and to all the house of Israel associated with him.'
**v17** Then join them together into one stick, so that they become one in your hand.

**v18** When your people ask you, 'Won't you explain to us what you mean by these?'
**v19** you are to tell them that this is what the Lord GOD says: 'I will take the stick of Joseph, which is in the hand of Ephraim, and the tribes of Israel associated with him, and I will put them together with the stick of Judah. I will make them into a single stick, and they will become one in My hand.'

**v20** When the sticks on which you write are in your hand and in full view of the people,
**v21** you are to tell them that this is what the Lord GOD says: 'I will take the Israelites out of the nations to which they have gone, and I will gather them from all around and bring them into their own land.
**v22** I will make them one nation in the land, on the mountains of Israel, and one king will rule over all of them. Then they will no longer be two nations and will never again be divided into two kingdoms.

**v23** They will no longer defile themselves with their idols or detestable images, or with any of their transgressions. I will save them from all their apostasies by which they sinned, [^3] and I will cleanse them. Then they will be My people, and I will be their God.
**v24** My servant David will be king over them, and there will be one shepherd for all of them. They will follow My ordinances and keep and observe My statutes.

**v25** They will live in the land that I gave to My servant Jacob, where your fathers lived. They will live there forever with their children and grandchildren, and My servant David will be their prince forever.
**v26** And I will make a covenant of peace with them; it will be an everlasting covenant. I will establish them and multiply them, and I will set My sanctuary among them forever.
**v27** My dwelling place [^4] will be with them; I will be their God, and they will be My people. [^5]
**v28** Then the nations will know that I the LORD sanctify Israel, when My sanctuary is among them forever.'"
[^1]: Or spirit; also in verses 6, 9, and 10 ( 37:5)
[^2]: Or branch; also in verses 17, 19, and 20 ( 37:16)
[^3]: Many Hebrew manuscripts (see also LXX); most Hebrew manuscripts all their dwelling places where they sinned ( 37:23)
[^4]: Or My tabernacle ( 37:27)
[^5]: Cited in 2 Corinthians 6:16 ( 37:27)

### Chapter 38

#### A Prophecy against Gog
**v1** And the word of the LORD came to me, saying,
**v2** "Son of man, set your face against Gog of the land of Magog, the chief prince of Meshech and Tubal. [^1] Prophesy against him
**v3** and declare that this is what the Lord GOD says: Behold, I am against you, O Gog, chief prince of Meshech and Tubal. [^2]
**v4** I will turn you around, put hooks in your jaws, and bring you out with all your army—your horses, your horsemen in full armor, and a great company armed with shields and bucklers, all brandishing their swords.
**v5** Persia, Cush, [^3] and Put will accompany them, all with shields and helmets,
**v6** as well as Gomer with all its troops, and Beth-togarmah from the far north with all its troops—the many nations with you.

**v7** Get ready; prepare yourself, you and all your company gathered around you; you will be their guard.
**v8** After a long time you will be summoned. In the latter years you will enter a land that has recovered from war, whose people were gathered from many nations to the mountains of Israel, which had long been desolate. They had been brought out from the nations, and all now dwell securely.
**v9** You and all your troops, and many peoples with you will go up, advancing like a thunderstorm; you will be like a cloud covering the land.

**v10** This is what the Lord GOD says: On that day, thoughts will arise in your mind, and you will devise an evil plan.
**v11** You will say, 'I will go up against a land of unwalled villages; I will come against a quiet people who dwell securely, all of them living without walls or bars or gates—
**v12** in order to seize the spoil and carry off the plunder, to turn a hand against the desolate places now inhabited and against a people gathered from the nations, who have acquired livestock and possessions and who live at the center of the land.'

**v13** Sheba and Dedan and the merchants of Tarshish with all its villages [^4] will ask, 'Have you come to capture the plunder? Have you assembled your hordes to carry away loot, to make off with silver and gold, to take cattle and goods, to seize great spoil?'

**v14** Therefore prophesy, son of man, and tell Gog that this is what the Lord GOD says: On that day when My people Israel are dwelling securely, will you not take notice of this? [^5]
**v15** And you will come from your place out of the far north—you and many peoples with you, all riding horses—a mighty horde, a huge army.
**v16** You will advance against My people Israel like a cloud covering the land. It will happen in the latter days, O Gog, that I will bring you against My land, so that the nations may know Me when I show Myself holy in you before their eyes.

**v17** This is what the Lord GOD says: Are you the one of whom I have spoken in former days through My servants, the prophets of Israel, who in those times prophesied for years that I would bring you against them?
**v18** Now on that day when Gog comes against the land of Israel, declares the Lord GOD, My wrath will flare up.

**v19** In My zeal and fiery rage I proclaim that on that day there will be a great earthquake in the land of Israel.
**v20** The fish of the sea, the birds of the air, the beasts of the field, every creature that crawls upon the ground, and all mankind on the face of the earth will tremble at My presence. The mountains will be thrown down, the cliffs will collapse, and every wall will fall to the ground.

**v21** And I will summon a sword against Gog on all My mountains, declares the Lord GOD, and every man's sword will be against his brother.
**v22** I will execute judgment upon him with plague and bloodshed. I will pour out torrents of rain, hailstones, fire, and sulfur on him and on his troops and on the many nations with him.
**v23** I will magnify and sanctify Myself, and I will reveal Myself in the sight of many nations. Then they will know that I am the LORD.
[^1]: Or of Magog, the prince of Rosh, Meshech, and Tubal ( 38:2)
[^2]: Or Gog, the prince of Rosh, Meshech, and Tubal ( 38:3)
[^3]: That is, the upper Nile region ( 38:5)
[^4]: Or young lions ( 38:13)
[^5]: LXX will you not rouse yourself? ( 38:14)

### Chapter 39

#### The Slaughter of Gog's Armies
**v1** "As for you, O son of man, prophesy against Gog and declare that this is what the Lord GOD says: Behold, I am against you, O Gog, chief prince of Meshech and Tubal. [^1]
**v2** I will turn you around, drive you along, bring you up from the far north, and send you against the mountains of Israel.
**v3** Then I will strike the bow from your left hand and dash down the arrows from your right hand.

**v4** On the mountains of Israel you will fall—you and all your troops and the nations with you. I will give you as food to every kind of ravenous bird and wild beast.
**v5** You will fall in the open field, for I have spoken, declares the Lord GOD.

**v6** I will send fire on Magog and on those who dwell securely in the coastlands, and they will know that I am the LORD.
**v7** So I will make My holy name known among My people Israel and will no longer allow it to be profaned. Then the nations will know that I am the LORD, the Holy One in Israel.
**v8** Yes, it is coming, and it will surely happen, declares the Lord GOD. This is the day of which I have spoken.

**v9** Then those who dwell in the cities of Israel will go out, kindle fires, and burn up the weapons—the bucklers and shields, the bows and arrows, the clubs and spears. For seven years they will use them for fuel.
**v10** They will not gather wood from the countryside or cut it from the forests, for they will use the weapons for fuel. They will loot those who looted them and plunder those who plundered them, declares the Lord GOD.

**v11** And on that day I will give Gog a burial place in Israel, the Valley of the Travelers, east of the Sea. [^2] It will block those who travel through, because Gog and all his hordes will be buried there. So it will be called the Valley of Hamon-gog. [^3]
**v12** For seven months the house of Israel will be burying them in order to cleanse the land.
**v13** All the people of the land will bury them, and it will bring them renown on the day I display My glory, [^4] declares the Lord GOD.

**v14** And men will be employed to continually pass through the land to cleanse it by burying the invaders who remain on the ground. At the end of the seven months they will begin their search.
**v15** As they pass through the land, anyone who sees a human bone will set up a pillar next to it, until the gravediggers have buried it in the Valley of Hamon-gog.
**v16** (Even the city will be named Hamonah. [^5]) And so they will cleanse the land.

**v17** And as for you, son of man, this is what the Lord GOD says: Call out to every kind of bird and to every beast of the field: 'Assemble and come together from all around to the sacrificial feast that I am preparing for you, a great feast on the mountains of Israel. There you will eat flesh and drink blood.
**v18** You will eat the flesh of the mighty and drink the blood of the princes of the earth as though they were rams, lambs, goats, and bulls—all the fattened animals of Bashan.
**v19** At the sacrifice I am preparing, you will eat fat until you are gorged and drink blood until you are drunk.
**v20** And at My table you will eat your fill of horses and riders, of mighty men and warriors of every kind,' declares the Lord GOD.
#### Israel to Be Restored

**v21** I will display My glory among the nations, and all the nations will see the judgment that I execute and the hand that I lay upon them.
**v22** From that day forward the house of Israel will know that I am the LORD their God.
**v23** And the nations will know that the house of Israel went into exile for their iniquity, because they were unfaithful to Me. So I hid My face from them and delivered them into the hands of their enemies, so that they all fell by the sword.
**v24** I dealt with them according to their uncleanness and transgressions, and I hid My face from them.

**v25** Therefore this is what the Lord GOD says: Now I will restore Jacob from captivity [^6] and will have compassion on the whole house of Israel, and I will be jealous for My holy name.
**v26** They will forget [^7] their disgrace and all the treachery they committed against Me, when they dwell securely in their land, with no one to frighten them.
**v27** When I bring them back from the peoples and gather them out of the lands of their enemies, I will show My holiness in them in the sight of many nations.
**v28** Then they will know that I am the LORD their God, when I regather them to their own land, not leaving any of them behind after their exile among the nations.
**v29** And I will no longer hide My face from them, for I will pour out My Spirit on the house of Israel, declares the Lord GOD."
[^1]: Or Gog, prince of Rosh, Meshech, and Tubal ( 39:1)
[^2]: Literally, the Sea ( 39:11)
[^3]: Hamon-gog means multitude of Gog. ( 39:11)
[^4]: Or and the day I display My glory will be a day of renown ( 39:13)
[^5]: Hamonah means multitude or horde. ( 39:16)
[^6]: Or restore the fortunes of Jacob ( 39:25)
[^7]: A few Hebrew manuscripts; MT They will bear ( 39:26)

### Chapter 40

#### The Man with a Measuring Rod
**v1** In the twenty-fifth year of our exile, at the beginning of the year, on the tenth day of the month—in the fourteenth year after Jerusalem had been struck down—on that very day the hand of the LORD was upon me, and He took me there.
**v2** In visions of God He took me to the land of Israel and set me on a very high mountain, on whose southern slope was a structure that resembled a city.

**v3** So He took me there, and I saw a man whose appearance was like bronze. He was standing in the gateway with a linen cord and a measuring rod in his hand.
**v4** "Son of man," he said to me, "look with your eyes, hear with your ears, and pay attention to everything I am going to show you, for that is why you have been brought here. Report to the house of Israel everything you see."
#### The East Gate

**v5** And I saw a wall surrounding the temple area. Now the length of the measuring rod in the man's hand was six long cubits [^1](each measuring a cubit and a handbreadth), and he measured the wall to be one rod thick and one rod high.

**v6** Then he came to the gate facing east and climbed its steps. He measured the threshold of the gate to be one rod deep. [^2]
**v7** Each gate chamber was one rod long and one rod wide, and there were five cubits [^3] between the gate chambers. The inner threshold of the gate by the portico facing inward was one rod deep.
**v8** Then he measured the portico of the gateway inside; [^4]
**v9** it was eight cubits deep, [^5] and its jambs were two cubits thick. [^6] And the portico of the gateway faced the temple.

**v10** There were three gate chambers on each side of the east gate, each with the same measurements, and the gateposts on either side also had the same measurements.
**v11** And he measured the width of the gateway entrance to be ten cubits, [^7] and its length was thirteen cubits. [^8]

**v12** In front of each gate chamber was a wall one cubit high, and the gate chambers were six cubits square.
**v13** Then he measured the gateway from the roof of one gate chamber to the roof of the opposite one; the distance was twenty-five cubits [^9] from doorway to doorway.

**v14** Next he measured the gateposts to be sixty cubits high. [^10] The gateway extended around to the gatepost of the courtyard.
**v15** And the distance from the entrance of the gateway to the far end of its inner portico was fifty cubits. [^11]

**v16** The gate chambers and their side pillars [^12] had beveled windows all around the inside of the gateway. The porticos also had windows all around on the inside. Each side pillar was decorated with palm trees.
#### The Outer Court

**v17** Then he brought me into the outer court, and there were chambers and a pavement laid out all around the court. Thirty chambers faced the pavement,
**v18** which flanked the gateways and corresponded to the length of the gates; this was the lower pavement.

**v19** Then he measured the distance from the front of the lower gateway to the outside of the inner court; it was a hundred cubits [^13] on the east side as well as on the north.
#### The North Gate

**v20** He also measured the length and width of the gateway of the outer court facing north.
**v21** Its three gate chambers on each side, its side pillars, and its portico all had the same measurements as the first gate: fifty cubits long and twenty-five cubits wide.
**v22** Its windows, portico, and palm trees had the same measurements as those of the gate facing east. Seven steps led up to it, with its portico opposite them.

**v23** There was a gate to the inner court facing the north gate, just as there was on the east. He measured the distance from gateway to gateway to be a hundred cubits.
#### The South Gate

**v24** Then he led me to the south side, and I saw a gateway facing south. He measured its side pillars and portico, and they had the same measurements as the others.
**v25** Both the gateway and its portico had windows all around, like the other windows. It was fifty cubits long and twenty-five cubits wide.
**v26** Seven steps led up to it, and its portico was opposite them; it had palm trees on its side pillars, one on each side.

**v27** The inner court also had a gate facing south, and he measured the distance from gateway to gateway toward the south to be a hundred cubits.
#### The Gates of the Inner Court

**v28** Next he brought me into the inner court through the south gate, and he measured the south gate; it had the same measurements as the others.
**v29** Its gate chambers, side pillars, and portico had the same measurements as the others. Both the gateway and its portico had windows all around; it was fifty cubits long and twenty-five cubits wide.
**v30** (The porticoes around the inner court were twenty-five cubits long and five cubits deep. [^14])
**v31** Its portico faced the outer court, and its side pillars were decorated with palm trees. Eight steps led up to it.

**v32** And he brought me to the inner court on the east side, and he measured the gateway; it had the same measurements as the others.
**v33** Its gate chambers, side pillars, and portico had the same measurements as the others. Both the gateway and its portico had windows all around. It was fifty cubits long and twenty-five cubits wide.
**v34** Its portico faced the outer court, and its side pillars were decorated with palm trees on each side. Eight steps led up to it.

**v35** Then he brought me to the north gate and measured it. It had the same measurements as the others,
**v36** as did its gate chambers, side pillars, and portico. It also had windows all around. It was fifty cubits long and twenty-five cubits wide.
**v37** Its portico [^15] faced the outer court, and its side pillars were decorated with palm trees on each side. Eight steps led up to it.
#### Eight Tables for Sacrifices

**v38** There was a chamber with a doorway by the portico [^16] in each of the inner gateways. There the burnt offering was to be washed.
**v39** Inside the portico of the gateway were two tables on each side, on which the burnt offerings, sin offerings, and guilt offerings were to be slaughtered.

**v40** Outside, as one goes up to the entrance of the north gateway, there were two tables on one side and two more tables on the other side of the gate's portico.
**v41** So there were four tables inside the gateway and four outside—eight tables in all—on which the sacrifices were to be slaughtered.

**v42** There were also four tables of dressed stone for the burnt offering, each a cubit and a half long, a cubit and a half wide, and a cubit high. [^17] On these were placed the utensils used to slaughter the burnt offerings and the other sacrifices.

**v43** The double-pronged hooks, [^18] each a handbreadth long, [^19] were fastened all around the inside of the room, and the flesh of the offering was to be placed on the tables.
#### Chambers for Ministry

**v44** Outside the inner gate, within the inner court, were two chambers, [^20] one beside the north gate and facing south, and another beside the south gate [^21] and facing north.

**v45** Then the man said to me: "The chamber that faces south is for the priests who keep charge of the temple,
**v46** and the chamber that faces north is for the priests who keep charge of the altar. These are the sons of Zadok, the only Levites who may approach the LORD to minister before Him."
#### The Inner Court

**v47** Next he measured the court. It was square, a hundred cubits long and a hundred cubits wide. And the altar was in front of the temple.

**v48** Then he brought me to the portico of the temple and measured the side pillars of the portico to be five cubits on each side. The width of the gateway was fourteen cubits and its sidewalls were three cubits on either side. [^22]
**v49** The portico was twenty cubits wide [^23] and twelve cubits deep, [^24] and ten steps led up to it. [^25] There were columns by the side pillars, one on each side.
[^1]: 6 long cubits, the length of the reed used for measuring, is approximately 10.5 feet or 3.2 meters; similarly in verses 6, 7, and 12. The long cubit of about 21 inches or 53.3 centimeters is the basic unit of length throughout Ezekiel 40 to 48. ( 40:5)
[^2]: Hebrew one reed deep, even one threshold, one reed deep. ( 40:6)
[^3]: 5 (long) cubits is approximately 8.75 feet or 2.7 meters; also in verses 30 and 48. ( 40:7)
[^4]: Literally the portico of the gateway inside, one rod ( 40:8)
